  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer4766534400301260250">For Will and Evanlyn, freedom has never felt so fleeing.<br/><br/>Still far from their homeland after escaping slavery in the icebound land of Skandia, the Ranger's apprentice and the princess's plan to return to Araluen is spoiled when Evanlyn is taken captive by a Temujai warrior.   <span id="freeText4766534400301260250" style="display:none">For Will and Evanlyn, freedom has never felt so fleeing.<br /><br />Still far from their homeland after escaping slavery in the icebound land of Skandia, the Ranger's apprentice and the princess's plan to return to Araluen is spoiled when Evanlyn is taken captive by a Temujai warrior. Though still weakened by the warmweed's toxic effects, Will employs his Ranger training to locate his friend, but an enemy scouting party has him fatally outnumbered. Will is certain death is close at hand, until old friends make a daring, last-minute rescue. The reunion is cut short, however, when they make a horrifying discovery: Skandia's borders have been breached by the entire Temujai army. And Araluen is next in their sights. <br /><br />If two kingdoms are to be saved, the unlikeliest of unions must be made. Will it hold long enough to vanquish a ruthless new enemy? Or will past tensions spell doom for all? <br /><br />The battles and drama are nonstop in Book Four of this hugely popular epic.</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_3815319').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_3815319').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_3815319').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/13750468?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex" href="/user/show/164794-alex">Alex</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer13750468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9116970836994355481">Holy Bananas!<br/><br/>Book Four in the Ranger's Apprentice not only makes up for the lack luster book Three, it left it my fists pumping in the air! Book Three basically set up the events for book Four, in which the ranger Halt and the warrior apprentice Horace were in search of the missing princess Evelyn and the ranger apprentice Will. But enough of the pleasantries and onto the action! Book Four, or the Battle for Skandia, is non stop action. Grab it now and enjoy! </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13084734267394447447" style="display:none">I'm sorry. Did you hear that noise? No? Well it was the sound of my heart exploding in sadness. A sound that will never be heard again in all time. <br /><br />At the end I decided who I shipped, and then my heart exploded in two. Will + Evelyn belong together. And now I'm extremely disappointed and scared to see if they will belong together. With both of them stuck on either side of the fence. Will being he is no longer her status. Evelyn being Rangers always keep to themselves. And me sitting here just waiting for my heart to explode. Then it did.<br /><br />Now I cannot give a good review, and probably will never be able to. Just know that I have been silenced in the beautifully sad closure of this book. I fear their lives will never be the same again.</span>

<div id="review_1532550131" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1532550131" />
    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365166675p2/13954899.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1532550131?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=older-kids-adults">older-kids-adults</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=speculative-or-fantastical-history">speculative-or-fantastical-history</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1532550131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer581482738877206011">Four solid stars. Told in 3rd person omniscient, there are only about 300 pages creating a swiftly flowing pace. (Long books wear me out). The plot is solid but not confusingly complex. The characters we met in earlier books return again, guarding each other's back, including Will, Horace, Evanlyn, Halt, Erak, etc. Their bond of friendship further develops, a spirit of camaraderie, loyalty, trust.<br/><br/>This series is classified as fantasy, but there are no fantastical elements in this particular entry</span>
  <span id="freeText581482738877206011" style="display:none">Four solid stars. Told in 3rd person omniscient, there are only about 300 pages creating a swiftly flowing pace. (Long books wear me out). The plot is solid but not confusingly complex. The characters we met in earlier books return again, guarding each other's back, including Will, Horace, Evanlyn, Halt, Erak, etc. Their bond of friendship further develops, a spirit of camaraderie, loyalty, trust.<br /><br />This series is classified as fantasy, but there are no fantastical elements in this particular entry (except one scene with a berserker killing rage). It's really more like an alternative history, where English-typecast characters (from Araluen) help the battle-axe toting Skandians (Vikings) repel an invasion of mongol-type invaders from the Eastern Steppes (the Temujai), light-calvary-archers led by a Khan-type chieftain.<br /><br />It was written for teens, but I enjoyed it. There is maybe too much time spent on battle scenes, but the tactics were interesting and the fight did not feel overwhelming. Kudos to the author for creating credible (not Mary Sue) action scenes with the young princess, Evanlyn / Cassandra.<br /><br />There is a good map and a fun app at the author's website: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.worldofjohnflanagan.com/ra">http://www.worldofjohnflanagan.com/ra</a>...<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="581482738877206011" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2007003142" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2007003142" />
    <a title="Johanna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58260626-johanna"><img alt="Johanna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473771266p2/58260626.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2007003142?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Johanna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Johanna" href="/user/show/58260626-johanna">Johanna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58260626-johanna?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2007003142" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18114683115506781677">The Battle for Skandia is the fourth book in the Ranger's Apprentice series.<br/>What can I say? These books are just incredibly relaxing for me to read. Flawed but endearing characters, easy but exciting plots. I don't have to think and can just enjoy it.<br/>Though in this particularly there were some things I would have liked differently. Most importantly I would have liked the book to deal with Will's trauma a bit more. He was enslaved, abused and drugged in the last book... I feel like he should have</span>
  <span id="freeText18114683115506781677" style="display:none">The Battle for Skandia is the fourth book in the Ranger's Apprentice series.<br />What can I say? These books are just incredibly relaxing for me to read. Flawed but endearing characters, easy but exciting plots. I don't have to think and can just enjoy it.<br />Though in this particularly there were some things I would have liked differently. Most importantly I would have liked the book to deal with Will's trauma a bit more. He was enslaved, abused and drugged in the last book... I feel like he should have some form of PTSD. Instead it was just kind of dropped and hardly ever mentioned again. That was a bit disappointing. I also feel like the series could use a bit more direction at this point. Not that it's not interesting but currently I'm missing an ultimate goal. What am I reading to? Is this series going to follow Will's life for the rest of eternity until his death? Just like some kind of road trip? Not that I won't read this, but still... A bit direction would be appreciated.<br />Apart from that, I'm still enjoying the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18114683115506781677" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17290119-rachel?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17290119-rachel?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1331615887" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6645839267213701918">There are few books that manage such a level of consistency - and that's a compliment, though it doesn't sound really like one. Normally in a series there are some good books, some not so good ones, great characters, characters that piss you off... the <i>Ranger's Apprentice</i> series has had nothing but a consistently engaging plotline, an incredible cast of loveable and a fascinating setting. It hasn't gotten boring once.<br/><br/>In this installment we get to know Erak more which I loved. Erak and Halt's dia</span>
  <span id="freeText6645839267213701918" style="display:none">There are few books that manage such a level of consistency - and that's a compliment, though it doesn't sound really like one. Normally in a series there are some good books, some not so good ones, great characters, characters that piss you off... the <i>Ranger's Apprentice</i> series has had nothing but a consistently engaging plotline, an incredible cast of loveable and a fascinating setting. It hasn't gotten boring once.<br /><br />In this installment we get to know Erak more which I loved. Erak and Halt's dialogue was hilarious. It was also fascinating to learn more about the Skandians. <br /><br />While the battle was a little long-winded, I think it was key. It gave Evanlyn the chance to grow in her character. After seeing everyone else doubt her abilities - at times, she even doubted herself - it was nice to see her grow in confidence and wow everyone with her hidden awesomeness. I'm intrigued about her and Horace's relationship and how it is going to progress over the rest of the series! <br /><br />I have to admit that I missed Will a little bit though. He still isn't back to his usual self (for most of the book) and he got a little weird towards the end. <br /><br />Overall, this was fantastic - just as I've learnt to expect from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/34049.John_Flanagan" title="John Flanagan" rel="nofollow noopener">John Flanagan</a>. I'm excited for the next book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6645839267213701918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8988628878107235072">3.5<br/><br/><br/><br/>This book was definitely the worst book in the series so far.<br/>I felt like the whole book was plainly just about war and tactics. Which is cool, there's nothing wrong with that, I actually enjoy reading about the characters discussing stragedy and stuff ike that, but not the whole book.   <span id="freeText8988628878107235072" style="display:none">3.5<br /><br /><br /><br />This book was definitely the worst book in the series so far.<br />I felt like the whole book was plainly just about war and tactics. Which is cool, there's nothing wrong with that, I actually enjoy reading about the characters discussing stragedy and stuff ike that, but not the whole book. I wanted too read more about the characters. Will, Horace and Evanlyn. I barely got that in this book.<br />I did like the last thirty pages though, so that's pretty good.<br />Overall this wasn't nearly as good as the last three, but still enjoyable, I guess.<br /><br />*Spoilers Below*<br /><br />And what about that skandian girl that told Will she wanted to carry his arrows for him? What happened to her? She wasn't mentioned one more time after that.<br /><br />Like I said before, I did like the ending. It was pretty nice seeing Will and the gang meet with everyone when they went back to Araluen. I actualy forgot that Halt was banished with everything going on. Happy his banishment was cut short.<br />Wait, so that ending means Will and Evanlyn/Cassandra are in love, right? I sort of knew all along. I mean, can you imagine Horace and Evanlyn/Cassandra together? There not a great match if you ask me.<br />So and okay book. This is a twelve book series--not including the prequels and sequels and the companion series-- so you gotta excpect that there will be a book you don't like in here. But I am still excited for the 5th book.</span>

<div id="review_1342262830" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1342262830" />
    <a title="C.P. Cabaniss" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9656259-c-p-cabaniss"><img alt="C.P. Cabaniss" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468698183p2/9656259.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1342262830?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.P. Cabaniss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.P. Cabaniss" href="/user/show/9656259-c-p-cabaniss">C.P. Cabaniss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=series-summer15">series-summer15</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=end-of-summer-cleanout15">end-of-summer-cleanout15</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=hangman-mmc15">hangman-mmc15</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=pagecount-mmc15">pagecount-mmc15</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=disney-blocks-mmc15">disney-blocks-mmc15</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9656259-c-p-cabaniss?shelf=mmc15">mmc15</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1342262830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer131250777501592049">This is the fourth installment in the Ranger's Apprentice series and takes place in Skandia, where Will and Evanlyn have been for nearly a year. When Halt and Horace arrive to rescue their friends, they must join forces with their enemies in order to return home. But enemies have a habit of becoming friends.<br/><br/>I was glad that Will was back and mostly himself in this novel because I missed him for the majority of the previous installment. And I loved his reunion with Halt. Their father/son relations</span>
  <span id="freeText131250777501592049" style="display:none">This is the fourth installment in the Ranger's Apprentice series and takes place in Skandia, where Will and Evanlyn have been for nearly a year. When Halt and Horace arrive to rescue their friends, they must join forces with their enemies in order to return home. But enemies have a habit of becoming friends.<br /><br />I was glad that Will was back and mostly himself in this novel because I missed him for the majority of the previous installment. And I loved his reunion with Halt. Their father/son relationship is beautiful and I love the bond that they have formed. His friendship with Horace was tested (slightly) and strengthened. <br /><br />This is really the first of the novels where there is a hint at future romance between any of the young characters. Evanlyn is friends with both Horace and Will and they both obviously care for her a great deal. It doesn't go too far, but it does introduce the possibility of relationships there. <br /><br />One thing I really enjoyed was how much we were able to see Evanlyn's strength. She didn't want to just sit on the sidelines and watch the men do all the dangerous work, she wanted to help. And her help was vital. It's nice to see girls be the heroes too, without taking away from the boys. The two can exist together. <br /><br />Another solid addition to this fun, adventurous series. I'm looking forward to continuing onward. </span>
  <a data-text-id="131250777501592049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_351082275" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351082275" />
    <a title="Joshua Letchford" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9553574-joshua-letchford"><img alt="Joshua Letchford" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390358870p2/9553574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351082275?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Joshua Letchford" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Joshua Letchford" href="/user/show/9553574-joshua-letchford">Joshua Letchford</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351082275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1348685088235102610">I really enjoyed the Ranger's Apprentice series as a light read, even as an older teenager. The books are very easy to pick up and Flanagan's style draws you into the story. <br/><br/>I gave this book five stars because it has probably the best battle-scene (it takes up nearly half of the book) I have ever found in fiction. Modern authors and movie-makers rarely understand medieval warfare. They are used to modern weapons like machine guns and artillery, so they use archers and catapults like automatic ri</span>
  <span id="freeText1348685088235102610" style="display:none">I really enjoyed the Ranger's Apprentice series as a light read, even as an older teenager. The books are very easy to pick up and Flanagan's style draws you into the story. <br /><br />I gave this book five stars because it has probably the best battle-scene (it takes up nearly half of the book) I have ever found in fiction. Modern authors and movie-makers rarely understand medieval warfare. They are used to modern weapons like machine guns and artillery, so they use archers and catapults like automatic rifles and cannons. The superhero complex encourages them to follow the exploits of a single hero who can plough through a battalion single-handedly (think the Jedi knights). <br /><br />Flanagan doesn't fall for any of that nonsense. His battle is interesting, clever, realistic and above all, plausible. The strategies the commanders use make sense, the tactics the warriors use are realistic, and oveall, I finished the book feeling like "that could have really happened". I reread this book just for that. But Flanagan doesn't get caught up in "getting it right"- he stil remembers to keep it personal. You aren't some bird flying over the battle watching it like a an all-knowing god; you watch the events unfold through the eyes of his beloved characters, especially Will, Horace and Halt. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1348685088235102610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer493350201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5295049715379028866">The fourth book in the Ranger's Apprentice series was an action filled adventure living up to the first three stories. I enjoyed the continuing story of Will and Evenlyn as they attempted to escape the Skandian city of Hallashome. Just as they seem to be free, the author throws another two plot twists at the reader and puts them back in harms way and the reader is bound to another gripping adventure. Halt, Horace, Evanlyn and Will all need to be at their best to take on the new challenges if the</span>
  <span id="freeText5295049715379028866" style="display:none">The fourth book in the Ranger's Apprentice series was an action filled adventure living up to the first three stories. I enjoyed the continuing story of Will and Evenlyn as they attempted to escape the Skandian city of Hallashome. Just as they seem to be free, the author throws another two plot twists at the reader and puts them back in harms way and the reader is bound to another gripping adventure. Halt, Horace, Evanlyn and Will all need to be at their best to take on the new challenges if the raiders from the steppes.<br /><br />I find the authors use of the Middle Ages, Europe, Asia and other cultures of the times quite interesting. It is easy to make connections to wonderful stories, sagas and histories while reading about Will in his adventures. It's a little like a simpler Lord of the Rings or even Robin Hood story which is action packed, full of fantasy, admirable characters and morals for all ages of readers. Certainly, the stories leave you wanting the next episode. I certainly can't wait to read book number 5.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5295049715379028866" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText2334081159431786379" style="display:none">Ooh, this one is where the series really starts to take an upward turn for the better. I'm going chronologically within the series, so I'm reading number seven after this, but I thoroughly enjoyed it. Oh, and it appealed to my rapidly growing interest in military history; the description of the titular Battle for Skandia is incredibly detailed and descriptive. This is one part where the series excels - the battles. To my knowledge the battle was fairly realistic as well, and how it was fought minor skirmishes, with one large pitched battle. Though it's a kids book, death and carnage of war isn't shied away from, which I appreciate. <br /><br />This is also where camaraderie really starts picking up; I love, love everyone's dynamic with each other. It gives me such warm fuzzy feelings inside.</span>

<div id="review_3432199354" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3432199354" />
    <a title="Di Maitland" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/112155925-di-maitland"><img alt="Di Maitland" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585661189p2/112155925.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3432199354?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Di Maitland" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Di Maitland" href="/user/show/112155925-di-maitland">Di Maitland</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39830132-oakleaf-bearers">review of another edition</a>

            Shelves:

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3432199354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15102398717866383888"><blockquote>"Are there bears in these mountains," he asked. His companion nodded.<br/>"Of course, but it's a bit early in the year for them to be moving around. Why?"<br/>Halt let go a long breath. "Just a vague hope, really. There's a chance that when the Temujai hear you crashing around in the trees, they might think you're a bear."<br/>Erak smiled with his mouth only, his eyes were as cold as the snow. "You're a very amusing fellow," he told Halt. "I'd like to brain you with my axe one of these days."<br/>"If you could mana</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15102398717866383888" style="display:none"><blockquote>"Are there bears in these mountains," he asked. His companion nodded.<br>"Of course, but it's a bit early in the year for them to be moving around. Why?"<br>Halt let go a long breath. "Just a vague hope, really. There's a chance that when the Temujai hear you crashing around in the trees, they might think you're a bear."<br>Erak smiled with his mouth only, his eyes were as cold as the snow. "You're a very amusing fellow," he told Halt. "I'd like to brain you with my axe one of these days."<br>"If you could manage to do it quietly, I'd almost welcome it," Halt said.<br><br>"I thought I told you to watch where you put your feet," he said accusingly.<br>Erak shrugged. "I did," he replied ruefully. "But while I was busy watching the ground, I hit that branch with my head. Broke it clean in two."<br>Halt raised his eyebrows. "I assume you're not talking about your head," he muttered<br>Erak frowned at the suggestion. "Of course not."<br>"More's the pity," Halt told him.</blockquote><br>The last of the library's Ranger's Apprentice audiobooks. I'm going to miss William Zappa and his dulcet British tones and extremely comical European accents.<br><br>As the winter snows melt, Will and Evanlyn find unexpected trouble near their mountain cabin. A scouting party of Tem'uj, nomadic, warrior-like peoples from the Eastern Steppes, take Evanlyn hostage. Fortunately, Halt and Horace arrive in the knick of time to save the day. Unfortunately, Jarl Erak also soon arrives on the scene. In return for their continued freedom, Halt agrees to scout the nearby Tem'uj army with Erak. But the Tem'uj army is far larger than either of them suspected, and it looks like, once the Temujai have conquered Skandia, they'll set their sights on Araluen. The only thing to do is to ensure they don't manage to conquer Skandia.<br><br>I adored the growing friendship between Halt and Erak. I've always imagined Erak looking a lot like Ragnar Lothbrok from Vikings.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1594410303i/29793360._SX540_.jpg" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Halt, meanwhile, is most definitely Aragorn.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1594410485i/29793367._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Both handsome in their own way; both well-respected and talented warriors and tacticians; and both morally upright, though not afraid to colour outside the lines. Their straight-faced banter made me laugh out loud at times. Hopefully we'll see more of Erak in the books to come (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2836109.Erak_s_Ransom__Ranger_s_Apprentice___7_" title="Erak's Ransom (Ranger's Apprentice, #7) by John Flanagan" rel="nofollow noopener">Erak's Ransom</a> would suggest so). <br><br>Will and Horace get their first taste of command, which they handle surprisingly well, and are finally beginning to discover girls *shock horror*. A small rivalry develops over Evanlyn's attentions - not a love triangle or anything, but certainly a spanner in the works. I'm not quite sure who I'd like to end up with her: Will, or Horace, or someone completely different. They're still children really (young 16-17 year olds) so we've got a while before it's likely to come to that.<br><br>And we finish back in Araluen at long last. Halt and Horace have been away a year, Will and Evanlyn many months more. I look forward to seeing what adventures they'll be taken on next. Fingers crossed the libraries reopen soon so I can find out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15102398717866383888" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8033917772928837867" style="display:none">Most of the book was about the battle, which I actually don't mind. Once again, I'm almost certain Flanagan had done lots of research because the terms and descriptions and battle strategies and whatnot seemed very realistic and believable. I'm not a huge fan of the writing style; it seemed to be a bit too explanatory in places I thought already were self explanatory if that makes sense. Nor am i a fan of the Skandians or the front cover :P But ah the ending!!!! The ending made the whole read worth it. So bittersweet. Looking forward to the next book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15950158936878942701">Book 4 is down, and it was a return to the action and adventure that was a little lacking in the last book. The young protagonists have grown both physically and mentally/emotionally. They've engaged in battle and endured hardship. The book ends on a positive note, leaving several areas for development in the following books. A good, fast series.</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7039679-ellen?shelf=audio">audio</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3368628890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6167243793743018017">So, this may be where I take a break with Ranger's Apprentice. I still really like the characters, but the plot hasn't seemed interesting to me for the past two books. It's probably due to the fact that it's mostly battles and I've never been one for reading about long battles. But if you do like that sort of thing, this series would be great for you.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11171674357013422949" style="display:none">In the last book, it last took place when Will and Evanlyn were kidnapped by the Skandians. Will is an apprentice ranger who is taught by Halt who is a ranger in the ranger corps. There are fifty rangers for each hold or castle. Rangers are like sheriffs in the modern world. Evanlyn is the daughter of the high king Duncan. The skandian kings servant Erak helped save Will and Evanlyn escape from Skandia. Will and Evanlyn escaped and stayed in this cabin for the winter. One day Evanlyn was going for hunting while Will slept and Evanlyn got kidnapped by the Temujai. The temujai are nomads who live in Temujai. They only go out of there area if they want to start a war by taking someones land. Thats when Will found out Evanlyn didnt come back and it was fifve hours later. So will followed the tracks for days until he reached a camp where they held Evanlyn. There were seven temujai and there weapon of choice is the long bow so is the rangers. Will was only armed with a bow so he moved closer. The temujai were about to kill Evanlyn until Will took a shot and missed. Then he saw another arrow fly passed him and he saw Halt who was there hidden in his camoflauge cloak. In four seconds he already killed five temujai. They went and saved and Evanlyn while Horace who was an apprentice knight killed two of the temujai easily. Erak was with them also because he need help from Halt. Halt had experience in wars and strategies thats why Erak wanted Halt to help them in the war against the temujai. Halt, Horace, Will, and Evanlyn went to skandia to fight off the temujai. They had an archer army of a hundred that was hidden under brush at a cliff. While the skandians held shields when they blocked off the arrows from the temujai. Will helped the skandian slaves aim and measure the range and distance and Evanlyn let Will know when they were ready. They took out half the temujai and they would've lost if will and halt hadn't thought of the archer idea. They barely survived until the temujai gave up when they lost more than half of there men. Temujai are hard to defeat becuase they are organized, trained, battle hardened, and full of stratigies. After that the skandians celebrated there victory and Halt, Horace, Will, and Evanlyn went back to Castle Araluen to celebrate with the king. </span>

  <span id="freeText6606716955886249218" style="display:none"> Evanlyn was tied to a thick pine, halfway down in the snow, watching the vicious Temujai about to slice her in two. An arrow suddenly burrowed into his wrist and he fell to his knees in pain. Suddenly three figures dashed from the forest and destroyed the Temujai camp taking just one prisnor.<br /><br /> As Will, a ranger's apprentice, Horace, a warrior apprentice, and Halt a full fledged ranger begin to leave the cold frozen land of Skandia they find a whole army of the marauding Temujai horseman ready to invade and destroy the entire realm and then directly after the realm of Araluen, our heroes' homeland. <br /><br /> In this book our heroes and the Skandians must cover up long fueds of war, and team up to fight back at the massive Temujai army, hoping to stop them in their tracks from conquering both kingdoms. This book's plot is outstanding with suspense always slowly but surely build, and many well thought strategies and at times hilarious twists and turns. <br /><br /> I reccomend this book to anyone that enjoys a great fantasy novel or anyone that has started the epic Ranger's Apprentice series. <br /><br /> Can the Skandians and Araulens bond together defeat the marauding Temujai or will they themselves be defeated? See for yourself in the newest addition to Ranger's Apprentice : The Battle For Skandia. </span>

<div id="review_83529286" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/83529286" />
    <a title="Mike (the Paladin)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2187043-mike-the-paladin"><img alt="Mike (the Paladin)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528431476p2/2187043.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/83529286?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mike (the Paladin)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mike (the Paladin)" href="/user/show/2187043-mike-the-paladin">Mike (the Paladin)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2187043-mike-the-paladin?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer83529286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer340187748335211370">The idea of a "Youth" book or a YA (Young Adult) book is a relatively new idea in literature, even as the idea of a set of books set aside as "children's books" is only a little older. I have recently read more of the genre YA noted above and I find there are a lot of wonderfully written and well plotted books in that genre. <br/><br/>I started the books in this series when I was looking for audio books for my wife who was ill at the time and spent a lot of time with audio books. I listened to these also </span>
  <span id="freeText340187748335211370" style="display:none">The idea of a "Youth" book or a YA (Young Adult) book is a relatively new idea in literature, even as the idea of a set of books set aside as "children's books" is only a little older. I have recently read more of the genre YA noted above and I find there are a lot of wonderfully written and well plotted books in that genre. <br /><br />I started the books in this series when I was looking for audio books for my wife who was ill at the time and spent a lot of time with audio books. I listened to these also and enjoyed them....at first. After the "capture motif" or "captive motif" was introduced I found my interest waning. Sadly (I thought) this one opened up with the beginnings of another captive story, happily he didn't drag this one out so much. I suppose I'd characterize this book as the Mongols meet the Northmen...and I won't say anymore lest I need to include a spoiler warning.<br /><br />While I still struggled to keep my interest centered in this book and found myself skipping and skimming it still had some good writing and while I didn't care for it as much (still) as I did the opening volumes of the "saga" I plan to go at least one more volume. (I have it out of the library already, so...why not) I hope that there may be an upturn coming. This one I give a 3 for the reliable writing, but it was close. So, if you're enjoying the series, good, but I think it slipped a little. </span>
  <a data-text-id="340187748335211370" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kayla Loewen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24783521-kayla-loewen"><img alt="Kayla Loewen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465325509p2/24783521.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743779865?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayla Loewen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayla Loewen" href="/user/show/24783521-kayla-loewen">Kayla Loewen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24783521-kayla-loewen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24783521-kayla-loewen?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24783521-kayla-loewen?shelf=absolute-ultimate-favorites">absolute-ultimate-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743779865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15848291347981558974">***SPOILER ALERT***<br/>I was both happy and sad when I finished reading this masterpiece. Happy because the book was just plain awesome, and although the ending was a touch melancholy, it was perfect. Sad because this book marks the end of Will's time as an apprentice to Halt (with the exception of book 7 of course, although he was practically full-fledged in that one.), and it also ends my favorite part of the series. Don't get me wrong, I absolutely love every book in this series, but books 1-4 ar</span>
  <span id="freeText15848291347981558974" style="display:none">***SPOILER ALERT***<br />I was both happy and sad when I finished reading this masterpiece. Happy because the book was just plain awesome, and although the ending was a touch melancholy, it was perfect. Sad because this book marks the end of Will's time as an apprentice to Halt (with the exception of book 7 of course, although he was practically full-fledged in that one.), and it also ends my favorite part of the series. Don't get me wrong, I absolutely love every book in this series, but books 1-4 are just.....extra special to me I guess. They carry a certain magic that the other books lack. But back to reviewing The Battle for Skandia! <br />I'm pretty sure I cried when Halt and Will were reunited; it couldn't have been more touching and awesome! It was so good to seem Will and Evanlyn safe with Halt and Horace again. <br />The plot twists with Slagor and the Temujai were brilliant, as was the way Halt and Will devised to over throw his plans. (Not to mention when Halt gets seasick, too funny!)<br />The battle=total epicness. Brilliantly written.<br />There wasn't a page of this book that bored me, I loved everything! Halt had so many great sarcastic replies; he's definitely the master of those!<br /> This book is one my treasures, and one of my all-time favorites! </span>
  <a data-text-id="15848291347981558974" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1160614201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8131321108663324952">A definite improvement compared to the last book. This book has a lot of good action scenes all the way through. I would almost say it's a little <i> too much</i> action because sometimes it dragged on a bit. It kind of feels like the third book and this one could easily have been just 1 book if they had less unnecessary scenes filling the pages. Still a good read, though.<br/><br/>Also, I still hope for some more interesting female characters as the story progresses. I like Evanlyn but there should be more than</span>
  <span id="freeText8131321108663324952" style="display:none">A definite improvement compared to the last book. This book has a lot of good action scenes all the way through. I would almost say it's a little <i> too much</i> action because sometimes it dragged on a bit. It kind of feels like the third book and this one could easily have been just 1 book if they had less unnecessary scenes filling the pages. Still a good read, though.<br /><br />Also, I still hope for some more interesting female characters as the story progresses. I like Evanlyn but there should be more than just one. </span>

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/54744885-the-king-of-the-west"><img alt="The King of the West (Path of the Ranger #7)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1596026730l/54744885._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/qnV81ZmbfPno7yHT2OlfJP3upqv6f89H9dMAtx2rtTEj7wh7Tikm0CICOa4lq+jRahdUmFkcVpEqQqzETVcTg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('s5Ugy0OCNVJMfPNQ/4d5Y3xh9fmPMbV89Q1fKUe8Qs2Js0kZ+Nz8OutXRzEIcnO8qj4SMUG8OxuucxmYiv+wVw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText11709653915411080330" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the GoodReads database with this name. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show_group/44217.Master_List_of_Author_Disambiguation_by_Spaces" rel="nofollow noopener">See this thread for more information</a>.</i><br /><br />For mysteries by this same author, see <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8307827.John_A__Flanagan" title="John A. Flanagan" rel="nofollow noopener">John A. Flanagan</a>.<br /><br />John Flanagan grew up in Sydney, Australia, hoping to be a writer. It wasn't until he wrote a highly uncomplimentary poem about a senior executive at the agency where he worked, however, that his talent was revealed. It turned out one of the company directors agreed with John's assessment of the executive, and happily agreed to train John in copywriting. <br /><br />After writing advertising copy for the next two decades, John teamed with an old friend to develop a television sitcom, Hey Dad!, which went on to air for eight years. <br /><br />John began writing Ranger's Apprentice for his son, Michael, ten years ago, and is still hard at work on the series. <br /><br />He currently lives in a suburb of Manly, Australia, with his wife. In addition to their son, they have two grown daughters and four grandsons.</span>

            if ($('bookCover_11309018').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_11309018').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
